The commando shots them down to go to the 2nd level.\r\n\r\nIn level-2 of Black Ops Sniper Strike the attackers come in armed vehicles and come out of it one-by-one shooting at the player. The vehicles cannot be destroyed which makes the game more difficult.\r\n\r\nIn level-3 Black Ops Sniper Strike the attackers come in helicopters and come down to ground by parachute.
